## 2026年水电站安全工作会议

发布日期: 发布时间：2026-03-28

<body><div data="datasource:20260328a79a3d004b1445c58c658843cae9ca3b" datatype="content"><meta name="ArticleTitle" content="2026年全国水电站安全工作会议在京召开"></div> <div data="datasource:20260328a79a3d004b1445c58c658843cae9ca3b" datatype="content"><meta name="PubDate" content="2026-03-28 10:43:13"></div> <div data="datasource:20260328a79a3d004b1445c58c658843cae9ca3b" datatype="content"><meta name="ContentSource" content="国家能源局"></div> <meta name="description" content="国家能源网"><meta name="keywords" content="国家能源网"><title data="datasource:20260328a79a3d004b1445c58c658843cae9ca3b" datatype="content">
            2026年全国水电站安全工作会议在京召开---国家能源局
        </title><link href="http://www.nea.gov.cn/static/default/css/public/master_nyj_v1.0.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"><link href="http://www.nea.gov.cn/static/default/css/article.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"><link href="http://www.nea.gov.cn/2015nyj/xinban/topbase.css" rel="stylesheet"><link href="http://www.nea.gov.cn/detail/css/cb_videoPlayer.css" rel="stylesheet"><script async="" src="//webd.home.news.cn/webdig.js?z=1"></script><script src="http://www.nea.gov.cn/static/default/js/public/jquery-1.9.1.min.js" type="text/javascript"></script><script language="javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {

            var lefttmp = new Image();
            lefttmp.src = "http://www.xinhuanet.com/photo/static/arr_left.cur";
            var righttmp = new Image();
            righttmp.src = "http://www.xinhuanet.com/photo/static/arr_right.cur";
            leng = $("a", $("#div_currpage")).length;

            if (leng != 0)
            //curr里有a标签==稿件不止一页
            {

                //看一共有多少个a标签
                leng = leng - 1;
                var nextLin = $("a", $("#div_currpage"))[leng].href; //对于多页的情况，取得下一页的地址
                var oneword = location.href + "#";
                if (nextLin == oneword) {
                    leng = leng - 1;
                    nextLin = $("a", $("#div_currpage"))[leng].href;
                }
                var currurl = location
                    .href; //当前页链接地址<meta http-equiv="expires" content="Sunday 26 October 2011 01:00 GMT" /> 

                var underpd = currurl.substring(currurl.indexOf("c_") + 2, currurl.indexOf(".htm"));
                if (underpd.indexOf("_") == -1) {

                    prevLink = location.href; //如果是文章首页，则左键仍是替换到本页面
                    nextLink = $("a", $("#div_currpage"))[0].href; //下一页的赋值
                    setTimeout("window.opener=null;window.location.href='" + nextLink + "'", 60000); //30秒跳转到下一页
                } else
                //是末页，http://news.xinhuanet.com/photo/2011-08/06/c_121822530.htm
                {
                    //当前页分页号判断
                    var currnum = currurl.indexOf(".htm"); //链接中第一次出现.htm的位置
                    var underlineindex = currurl.lastIndexOf("_") + 1; //下划线甄别标识，第一页则不是下划线
                    //下一页的分页号
                    var nextnum = nextLin.indexOf(".htm"); //链接中第一次出现.htm的位置
                    var underlinenext = nextLin.lastIndexOf("_") + 1; //下划线甄别标识，第一页则不是下划线
                    var undernum = nextLin.substr(nextLin.indexOf("c_")).split("_").length - 1;

                    var temp = currurl.substring(underlineindex, currnum); //当前页的分页号
                    var nexttemp = nextLin.substring(underlinenext, nextnum); //最后a标签的分页号
                    var boolx = parseInt(temp, 10) > parseInt(nexttemp, 10);

                    if ((boolx) || (undernum == 1)) //末页

                    {

                        if ($("img", $("a", $("#content"))).length == 0) //没有带链接的图片

                        {
                            prevLink = nextLin;
                            if (undernum == 1) {
                                nextLink = nextLin;
                            } else {
                                nextLink = prevLink.substr(0, (prevLink.lastIndexOf("_"))) + ".htm";
                            }
                            setTimeout("window.opener=null;window.location.href='" + nextLink + "'",
                                60000); //30秒跳转到下一页
                        } else //末页正文图片有链接
                        {
                            prevLink = nextLin;
                            nextLink = $("a", $("#content"))[0].href; //把正文第一个带链接的链接地址赋给下一页
                        }

                    } else //不是末页
                    {

                        prevLink = $("a", $("#div_currpage"))[0].href; //把正文第一个带链接的链接地址赋给下一页
                        nextLink = nextLin; //把正文最后一个带链接的链接地址赋给下一页
                    }

                }
            } else
            //只有一页
            {
                prevLink = location.href;
                nextLink = location.href;
            }

            document.onkeydown = pageEvent;

            function pageEvent(evt) {
                evt = evt || window.event;
                var key = evt.which || evt.keyCode;
                if (key == 37) location = prevLink;
                if (key == 39) location = nextLink;
            };

            var lefturl = prevLink;
            var righturl = nextLink;
            var imgurl = righturl;

            $("#content img").each(function () {
                var width = $(this).width();
                var thisImage = $(this);
                //alert("01");
                $(thisImage)[0].onmousemove = function () {

                    if (event.offsetX < width / 2) {

                        this.style.cursor = 'url(' + lefttmp.src + '),auto';
                        imgurl = lefturl;
                    } else {

                        this.style.cursor = 'url(' + righttmp.src + '),auto';
                        imgurl = righturl;
                    }

                }

                $(thisImage)[0].onmouseup = function () {
                    top.location = imgurl;

                }
            });

        });

                        2026年全国水电站安全工作会议在京召开
                    </div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <span class="times">
                        发布时间：2026-03-28
                    </span> <span class="author">

                    </span> <span class="switchsize"><b class="bigger">大</b><b class="medium">中</b><b class="smaller">小</b></span> <div class="arrow"></div></div> <div class="article-box"><div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div id="detail" data="datasource:20260328a79a3d004b1445c58c658843cae9ca3b" datatype="content"><div class="article-content"><span id="detailContent"><p>  3月25日，国家能源局召开2026年全国水电站安全工作会议，总结“十四五”水电站安全工作，分析“十五五”水电站安全面临的形势，部署“十五五”及2026年水电站安全重点工作。国家能源局党组成员、副局长何洋出席会议并讲话。</p><section style="text-align: center;"><img id="iJM2lHJYlYRGwRq3JyCL" class="rich_pages wxw-img" style="height: auto !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 677px !important;" src="20260328a79a3d004b1445c58c658843cae9ca3b_20260328beffebbf92894448bb53656433262f99.jpeg" alt="图片" data-aistatus="1" data-imgfileid="504679331" data-ratio="0.6666666666666666" data-s="300,640" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" data-original-style="height: auto !important;" data-index="1" data-sec-load-status="2" data-report-img-idx="1" data-material-id="26032800508142" data-name="20260328beffebbf92894448bb53656433262f99.jpeg"></section><p>  会议要求，电力行业要深入贯彻党的二十大和二十届历次全会精神，认真落实四中全会部署，准确把握习近平总书记关于能源安全、防汛抗旱、防灾减灾的重要指示批示精神，按照党中央、国务院关于安全生产工作的决策部署，压实水电站安全责任，夯实水电站本质安全基础，提升水电站安全管理水平，未雨绸缪做好防汛度汛准备，全力推动水电站安全工作再上新台阶。</p><p>  国家能源局监管总监，有关司、大坝中心、可靠性和质监中心，全国电力安全生产委员会各企业成员单位有关负责同志在主会场参加会议。各省（自治区、直辖市）和新疆生产建设兵团能源主管部门、国家能源局各派出机构有关负责同志在分会场视频参会。</p></span></div></div> <div class="back-top"><a href="javascript:void(0)" title="返回顶部" style="display: none;">返回顶部</a></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div></div> <div class="article-other"><div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="clear"></div></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div> <div class="hr_10"></div></div></div> <script src="http://www.nea.gov.cn/2015nyj/xinban/bottom.js" type="text/javascript"></script><meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html;
